    <div class="overview">
      <span class="short">
                  Aside from a love for hoops, it would seem that Lucas and Nathan are two young men with little in co... <a href="#" class="overview-more-link">More</a>
              </span>
      <span class="long" itemprop="description">Aside from a love for hoops, it would seem that Lucas and Nathan are two young men with little in common, but they are bound by the dark secret that they share the same father. Nathan is the star of the high school basketball team and local town hero, while Lucas is the only child of a single working mom. Now the two boys&#039; lives collide when a twist of fate puts Lucas on Nathan&#039;s team and the half-brothers compete, not only for control of the court, but also for the heart of Nathan&#039;s beautiful girlfriend Peyton.</span>
    </div>

	<script>
		// fb login function
		function fbConnect() {
			FB.login(function(response) {
				// handle the response
				if (response.authResponse) {
					$('#connect_fb_access_token').val(response.authResponse.accessToken);
					$('#connect-form').submit();
				}
				else {
					//TODO: handle error
					console.log('User cancelled login or did not fully authorize.');
				}
			}, {scope: 'email'});

			return false;
		}

		// twitter connect function
		function twitterConnect() {
			$('#connect_twitter_oauth').val(true);
			$('#connect-form').submit();

			return false;
		}

		// tvst connect function
		function tvstConnect() {
			$('#connect_tvst').val(true);
			$('#connect-form').submit();

			return false;
		}
	</script>
